float:left; padding:0 auto; border-style:none; clear:both; text-align:center; width:20.5em">\n        <a href="/wiki/Cartesian_coordinate_system#One_dimension" title="Cartesian coordinate system">\n         Axis scale\n        </a>\n        :\n        <a href="/wiki/Geologic_time_scale" title="Geologic time scale">\n         billions of years ago\n        </a>\n        .\n        <br/>\n        <small>\n         Also see:\n         <i>\n          <a href="/wiki/Template:Human_timeline" title="Template:Human timeline">\n           Human timeline\n          </a>\n         </i>\n         and\n         <i>\n          <a href="/wiki/Template:Life_timeline" title="Template:Life timeline">\n           Life timeline\n          </a>\n         </i>\n        </small>\n       </div>\n      </div>\n      <div class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable" role="note">\n       See also:\n       <a href="/wiki/Extraterrestrial_life" title="Extraterrestrial life">\n        Extraterrestrial life\n       </a>\n      </div>\n      <p>\n       The systematic search for possible life outside Earth is a valid multidisciplinary scientific endeavor.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-108">\n        <a href="#cite_note-108">\n         [108]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       However, hypotheses and predictions as to its existence and origin vary widely, and at the present, the development of hypotheses firmly grounded on science may be considered astrobiology\'s most concrete practical application. It has been proposed that\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Viruses" title="Viruses">\n        viruses\n       </a>\n       are likely to be encountered on other life-bearing planets.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Astro-20130814_109-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-Astro-20130814-109">\n         [109]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <h3>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Research_outcomes">\n        Research outcomes\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Astrobiology&amp;action=edit&amp;section=13" title="Edit section: Research outcomes">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <div class="thumb tleft">\n       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:202px;">\n        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:951_Gaspra.jpg">\n         <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="785" data-file-width="945" height="166" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/81/951_Gaspra.jpg/200px-951_Gaspra.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/81/951_Gaspra.jpg/300px-951_Gaspra.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/81/951_Gaspra.jpg/400px-951_Gaspra.jpg 2x" width="200"/>\n        </a>\n        <div class="thumbcaption">\n         <div class="magnify">\n          <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:951_Gaspra.jpg" title="Enlarge">\n          </a>\n         </div>\n         Asteroid(s) may have transported life to\n         <a href="/wiki/Earth" title="Earth">\n          Earth\n         </a>\n         .\n        </div>\n       </div>\n      </div>\n      <p>\n       As of 2017\n       <sup class="plainlinks noprint asof-tag update" style="display:none;">\n        <a class="external text" href="//en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Astrobiology&amp;action=edit">\n         [update]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       , no evidence of extraterrestrial life has been identified.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-110">\n        <a href="#cite_note-110">\n         [110]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Examination of the\n       <a href="/wiki/Allan_Hills_84001" title="Allan Hills 84001">\n        Allan Hills 84001\n       </a>\n       meteorite, which was recovered in\n       <a href="/wiki/Antarctica" title="Antarctica">\n        Antarctica\n       </a>\n       in 1984 and originated from\n       <a href="/wiki/Mars" title="Mars">\n        Mars\n       </a>\n       , is thought by\n       <a href="/wiki/David_S._McKay" title="David S. McKay">\n        David McKay\n       </a>\n       , as well as few other scientists, to contain\n       <a href="/wiki/Fossil#Microfossils" title="Fossil">\n        microfossils\n       </a>\n       of extraterrestrial origin; this interpretation is controversial.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-disbelief_111-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-disbelief-111">\n         [111]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-life_112-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-life-112">\n         [112]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-McKay_113-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-McKay-113">\n         [113]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       <a href="/wiki/Yamato_000593" title="Yamato 000593">\n        Yamato 000593\n       </a>\n       , the\n       <a href="/wiki/List_of_Martian_meteorites#List" title="List of Martian meteorites">\n        second largest\n       </a>\n       <a href="/wiki/Meteorite" title="Meteorite">\n        meteorite\n       </a>\n       from\n       <a href="/wiki/Mars" title="Mars">\n        Mars\n       </a>\n       , was found on Earth in 2000. At a microscopic level,\n       <a href="/wiki/Martian_spherules" title="Martian spherules">\n        spheres\n       </a>\n       are found in the meteorite that are rich in\n       <a href="/wiki/Carbon" title="Carbon">\n        carbon\n       </a>\n       compared to surrounding areas that lack such spheres. The carbon-rich spheres may have been formed by\n       <a href="/wiki/Biotic_material" title="Biotic material">\n        biotic activity\n       </a>\n       according to some NASA scientists.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-NASA-20140227_114-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-NASA-20140227-114">\n         [114]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-AJ-20140219_115-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-AJ-20140219-115">\n         [115]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-SP-20140228_116-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-SP-20140228-116">\n         [116]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <p>\n       On 5 March 2011,\n       <a href="/wiki/Richard_B._Hoover" title="Richard B. Hoover">\n        Richard B. Hoover\n       </a>\n       , a scientist with the\n       <a href="/wiki/Marshall_Space_Flight_Center" title="Marshall Space Flight Center">\n        Marshall Space Flight Center\n       </a>\n       , speculated on the finding of alleged microfossils similar to\n       <a href="/wiki/Cyanobacteria" title="Cyanobacteria">\n        cyanobacteria\n       </a>\n       in\n       <a href="/wiki/CI1_fossils" title="CI1 fossils">\n        CI1\n       </a>\n       carbonaceous\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Meteorites" title="Meteorites">\n        meteorites\n       </a>\n       in the\n       <a href="/wiki/Fringe_science" title="Fringe science">\n        fringe\n       </a>\n       <i>\n        <a href="/wiki/Journal_of_Cosmology" title="Journal of Cosmology">\n         Journal of Cosmology\n        </a>\n       </i>\n       , a story widely reported on by\n       <a href="/wiki/Mainstream_media" title="Mainstream media">\n        mainstream media\n       </a>\n       .\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Tenney_117-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-Tenney-117">\n         [117]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Hoover_118-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-Hoover-118">\n         [118]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       However, NASA formally distanced itself from Hoover\'s claim.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-119">\n        <a href="#cite_note-119">\n         [119]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       According to American astrophysicist\n       <a href="/wiki/Neil_deGrasse_Tyson" title="Neil deGrasse Tyson">\n        Neil deGrasse Tyson\n       </a>\n       : "At the moment, life on Earth is the only known life in the universe, but there are compelling arguments to suggest we are not alone."\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-120">\n        <a href="#cite_note-120">\n         [120]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <dl>\n       <dt>\n        Extreme environments on Earth\n       </dt>\n      </dl>\n      <p>\n       On 17 March 2013, researchers reported that\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Microbes" title="Microbes">\n        microbial life forms\n       </a>\n       thrive in the\n       <a href="/wiki/Mariana_Trench" title="Mariana Trench">\n        Mariana Trench\n       </a>\n       , the deepest spot on the Earth.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-LS-20130317_121-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-LS-20130317-121">\n         [121]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-NG-20130317_122-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-NG-20130317-122">\n         [122]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Other researchers reported that microbes thrive inside rocks up to 1,900 feet (580\xc2\xa0m) below the sea floor under 8,500 feet (2,600\xc2\xa0m) of ocean off the coast of the northwestern United States.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-LS-20130317_121-1">\n        <a href="#cite_note-LS-20130317-121">\n         [121]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-LS-20130314_123-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-LS-20130314-123">\n         [123]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       According to one of the researchers, "You can find microbes everywhere\xe2\x80\x94they\'re extremely adaptable to conditions, and survive wherever they are."\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-LS-20130317_121-2">\n        <a href="#cite_note-LS-20130317-121">\n         [121]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       These finds expand the potential habitability of certain niches of other planets.\n      </p>\n      <dl>\n       <dt>\n        Methane\n       </dt>\n      </dl>\n      <p>\n       In 2004, the spectral signature of\n       <a href="/wiki/Methane" title="Methane">\n        methane\n       </a>\n       (\n       <span class="chemf nowrap">\n        CH\n        <span style="display:inline-block;margin-bottom:-0.3em;vertical-align:-0.4em;line-height:1em;font-size:80%;text-align:left">\n         <br/>\n         4\n        </span>\n       </span>\n       ) was detected in the Martian atmosphere by both Earth-based telescopes as well as by the\n       <a href="/wiki/Mars_Express" title="Mars Express">\n        Mars Express\n       </a>\n       orbiter. Because of\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Solar_radiation" title="Solar radiation">\n        solar radiation\n       </a>\n       and\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Cosmic_radiation" title="Cosmic radiation">\n        cosmic radiation\n       </a>\n       , methane is predicted to disappear from the Martian atmosphere within several years, so the gas must be actively replenished in order to maintain the present concentration.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-results_124-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-results-124">\n         [124]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-fourier-spec_125-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-fourier-spec-125">\n         [125]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       The\n       <a href="/wiki/Curiosity_(rover)" title="Curiosity (rover)">\n        <i>\n         Curiosity\n        </i>\n       </a>\n       rover will perform precision measurements of oxygen and carbon\n       <a href="/wiki/Isotope" title="Isotope">\n        isotope\n       </a>\n       ratios in carbon dioxide (CO\n       <sub>\n        2\n       </sub>\n       ) and methane (CH\n       <sub>\n        4\n       </sub>\n       ) in the\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Atmosphere_of_mars#Methane" title="Atmosphere of mars">\n        atmosphere of Mars\n       </a>\n       in order to distinguish between a\n       <a href="/wiki/Geochemistry" title="Geochemistry">\n        geochemical\n       </a>\n       and a\n       <a href="/wiki/Biology" title="Biology">\n        biological\n       </a>\n       origin.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-SAM_126-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-SAM-126">\n         [126]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-127">\n        <a href="#cite_note-127">\n         [127]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-128">\n        <a href="#cite_note-128">\n         [128]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <dl>\n       <dt>\n        Planetary systems\n       </dt>\n      </dl>\n      <p>\n       It is possible that some exoplanets may have moons with solid surfaces or liquid oceans that are hospitable. Most of the planets so far discovered outside the Solar System are hot gas giants thought to be inhospitable to life, so it is not yet known whether the Solar System, with a warm, rocky, metal-rich inner planet such as Earth, is of an aberrant composition. Improved detection methods and increased observation time will undoubtedly discover more planetary systems, and possibly some more like ours. For example, NASA\'s\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Kepler_Mission" title="Kepler Mission">\n        Kepler Mission\n       </a>\n       seeks to discover Earth-sized planets around other stars by measuring minute changes in the star\'s\n       <a href="/wiki/Light_curve" title="Light curve">\n        light curve\n       </a>\n       as the planet passes between the star and the spacecraft. Progress in\n       <a href="/wiki/Infrared_astronomy" title="Infrared astronomy">\n        infrared astronomy\n       </a>\n       and\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Submillimeter_astronomy" title="Submillimeter astronomy">\n        submillimeter astronomy\n       </a>\n       has revealed the constituents of other\n       <a href="/wiki/Star_system" title="Star system">\n        star systems\n       </a>\n       .\n      </p>\n      <dl>\n       <dt>\n        Planetary habitability\n       </dt>\n      </dl>\n      <div class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable" role="note">\n       Main article:\n       <a href="/wiki/Planetary_habitability" title="Planetary habitability">\n        Planetary habitability\n       </a>\n      </div>\n      <p>\n       Efforts to answer questions such as the abundance of potentially habitable planets in\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Habitable_zone" title="Habitable zone">\n        habitable zones\n       </a>\n       and chemical precursors have had much success. Numerous\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Extrasolar_planet" title="Extrasolar planet">\n        extrasolar planets\n       </a>\n       have been detected using the\n       <a href="/wiki/Doppler_spectroscopy" title="Doppler spectroscopy">\n        wobble method\n       </a>\n       and\n       <a href="/wiki/Methods_of_detecting_exoplanets#Transit_photometry" title="Methods of detecting exoplanets">\n        transit method\n       </a>\n       , showing that planets around other\n       <a href="/wiki/Star" title="Star">\n        stars\n       </a>\n       are more numerous than previously postulated. The first Earth-sized extrasolar planet to be discovered within its star\'s habitable zone is\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Gliese_581_c" title="Gliese 581 c">\n        Gliese 581 c\n       </a>\n       .\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Gliese_129-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-Gliese-129">\n         [129]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <h2>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Missions">\n        Missions\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Astrobiology&amp;action=edit&amp;section=14" title="Edit section: Missions">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h2>\n      <p>\n       Research into the environmental limits of life and the workings of extreme\n       <a href="/wiki/Ecosystem" title="Ecosystem">\n        ecosystems\n       </a>\n       is ongoing, enabling researchers to better predict what planetary environments might be most likely to harbor life. Missions such as the\n       <a href="/wiki/Phoenix_(spacecraft)" title="Phoenix (spacecraft)">\n        <i>\n         Phoenix\n        </i>\n        lander\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <a href="/wiki/Mars_Science_Laboratory" title="Mars Science Laboratory">\n        Mars Science Laboratory\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <a href="/wiki/ExoMars" title="ExoMars">\n        ExoMars\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <a href="/wiki/Mars_2020" title="Mars 2020">\n        Mars 2020\n       </a>\n       rover to Mars, and the\n       <a href="/wiki/Cassini%E2%80%93Huygens" title="Cassini\xe2\x80\x93Huygens">\n        <i>\n         Cassini\n        </i>\n        probe\n       </a>\n       to\n       <a href="/wiki/Saturn" title="Saturn">\n        Saturn\n       </a>\n       \'s moons aim to further explore the possibilities of life on other planets in the Solar System.\n      </p>\n      <h3>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Viking_program">\n        Viking program\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Astrobiology&amp;action=edit&amp;section=15" title="Edit section: Viking program">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <div class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable" role="note">\n       Main article:\n       <a href="/wiki/Viking_lander_biological_experiments" title="Viking lander biological experiments">\n        Viking lander biological experiments\n       </a>\n      </div>\n      <div class="thumb tright">\n       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;">\n        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Sagan_Viking.jpg">\n         <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="2468" data-file-width="3678" height="148" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/e8/Sagan_Viking.jpg/220px-Sagan_Viking.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/e8/Sagan_Viking.jpg/330px-Sagan_Viking.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/e8/Sagan_Viking.jpg/440px-Sagan_Viking.jpg 2x" width="220"/>\n        </a>\n        <div class="thumbcaption">\n         <div class="magnify">\n          <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Sagan_Viking.jpg" title="Enlarge">\n          </a>\n         </div>\n         <a href="/wiki/Carl_Sagan" title="Carl Sagan">\n          Carl Sagan\n         </a>\n         posing with a model of the Viking Lander.\n        </div>\n       </div>\n      </div>\n      <p>\n       The two\n       <a href="/wiki/Viking_program" title="Viking program">\n        Viking landers\n       </a>\n       each carried four types of biological experiments to the surface of Mars in the late 1970s. These were the only Mars landers to carry out experiments looking specifically for\n       <a href="/wiki/Metabolism" title="Metabolism">\n        metabolism\n       </a>\n       by current microbial\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Life_on_Mars_(planet)" title="Life on Mars (planet)">\n        life on Mars\n       </a>\n       . The landers used a robotic arm to collect soil samples into sealed test containers on the craft. The two landers were identical, so the same tests were carried out at two places on Mars\' surface;\n       <a href="/wiki/Viking_1" title="Viking 1">\n        Viking 1\n       </a>\n       near the equator and\n       <a href="/wiki/Viking_2" title="Viking 2">\n        Viking 2\n       </a>\n       further north.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Chambers_130-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-Chambers-130">\n         [130]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       The result was inconclusive,\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-131">\n        <a href="#cite_note-131">\n         [131]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       and is still disputed by some scientists.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Bianciardi-2012_132-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-Bianciardi-2012-132">\n         [132]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Discovery-20120412_133-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-Discovery-20120412-133">\n         [133]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Navarro_134-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-Navarro-134">\n         [134]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Paepe_135-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-Paepe-135">\n         [135]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <h3>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Beagle_2">\n        Beagle 2\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Astrobiology&amp;action=edit&amp;section=16" title="Edit section: Beagle 2">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <div class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable" role="note">\n       Main article:\n       <a href="/wiki/Beagle_2" title="Beagle 2">\n        Beagle 2\n       </a>\n      </div>\n      <div class="thumb tright">\n       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;">\n        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Beagle_2_replica.jpg">\n         <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="3000" data-file-width="4000" height="165" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/a8/Beagle_2_replica.jpg/220px-Beagle_2_replica.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/a8/Beagle_2_replica.jpg/330px-Beagle_2_replica.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/a8/Beagle_2_replica.jpg/440px-Beagle_2_replica.jpg 2x" width="220"/>\n        </a>\n        <div class="thumbcaption">\n         <div class="magnify">\n          <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Beagle_2_replica.jpg" title="Enlarge">\n          </a>\n         </div>\n         Replica of the 33.2 kg\n         <i>\n          Beagle-2\n         </i>\n         lander\n        </div>\n       </div>\n      </div>\n      <div class="thumb tright">\n       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;">\n        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Mars_Science_Laboratory_Curiosity_rover.jpg">\n         <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="1406" data-file-width="2500" height="124" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/a9/Mars_Science_Laboratory_Curiosity_rover.jpg/220px-Mars_Science_Laboratory_Curiosity_rover.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/a9/Mars_Science_Laboratory_Curiosity_rover.jpg/330px-Mars_Science_Laboratory_Curiosity_rover.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/a9/Mars_Science_Laboratory_Curiosity_rover.jpg/440px-Mars_Science_Laboratory_Curiosity_rover.jpg 2x" width="220"/>\n        </a>\n        <div class="thumbcaption">\n         <div class="magnify">\n          <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Mars_Science_Laboratory_Curiosity_rover.jpg" title="Enlarge">\n          </a>\n         </div>\n         <a href="/wiki/Mars_Science_Laboratory" title="Mars Science Laboratory">\n          Mars Science Laboratory\n         </a>\n         rover concept artwork\n        </div>\n       </div>\n      </div>\n      <p>\n       <i>\n        Beagle 2\n       </i>\n       was an unsuccessful\n       <a href="/wiki/United_Kingdom" title="United Kingdom">\n        British\n       </a>\n       Mars lander that formed part of the\n       <a href="/wiki/European_Space_Agency" title="European Space Agency">\n        European Space Agency\n       </a>\n       \'s 2003\n       <a href="/wiki/Mars_Express" title="Mars Express">\n        Mars Express\n       </a>\n       mission. Its primary purpose was to search for signs of\n       <a href="/wiki/Life_on_Mars" title="Life on Mars">\n        life on Mars\n       </a>\n       , past or present. Although it landed safely, it was unable to correctly deploy its solar panels and telecom antenna.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-136">\n        <a href="#cite_note-136">\n         [136]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <h3>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="EXPOSE">\n        EXPOSE\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Astrobiology&amp;action=edit&amp;section=17" title="Edit section: EXPOSE">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <div class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable" role="note">\n       Main article:\n       <a href="/wiki/EXPOSE" title="EXPOSE">\n        EXPOSE\n       </a>\n      </div>\n      <p>\n       <a href="/wiki/EXPOSE" title="EXPOSE">\n        EXPOSE\n       </a>\n       is a multi-user facility mounted in 2008 outside the\n       <a href="/wiki/International_Space_Station" title="International Space Station">\n        International Space Station\n       </a>\n       dedicated to astrobiology.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Rabbow_137-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-Rabbow-137">\n         [137]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Experimental_methods_138-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-Experimental_methods-138">\n         [138]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       EXPOSE was developed by the\n       <a href="/wiki/European_Space_Agency" title="European Space Agency">\n        European Space Agency\n       </a>\n       (ESA) for\n       <a href="/wiki/Spaceflight" title="Spaceflight">\n        long-term spaceflights\n       </a>\n       that allow exposure of\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Organic_chemical" title="Organic chemical">\n        organic chemicals\n       </a>\n       and biological samples to\n       <a href="/wiki/Outer_space" title="Outer space">\n        outer space\n       </a>\n       in\n       <a href="/wiki/Low_Earth_orbit" title="Low Earth orbit">\n        low Earth orbit\n       </a>\n       .\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-home_139-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-home-139">\n         [139]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <h3>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Mars_Science_Laboratory">\n        Mars Science Laboratory\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Astrobiology&amp;action=edit&amp;section=18" title="Edit section: Mars Science Laboratory">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <div class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable" role="note">\n       Main article:\n       <a href="/wiki/Mars_Science_Laboratory" title="Mars Science Laboratory">\n        Mars Science Laboratory\n       </a>\n      </div>\n      <p>\n       The Mars Science Laboratory (MSL) mission landed the\n       <a href="/wiki/Curiosity_(rover)" title="Curiosity (rover)">\n        <i>\n         Curiosity\n        </i>\n       </a>\n       <a href="/wiki/Rover_(space_exploration)" title="Rover (space exploration)">\n        rover\n       </a>\n       that is currently in operation on\n       <a href="/wiki/Mars" title="Mars">\n        Mars\n       </a>\n       .\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-MSLNameWebsite_140-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-MSLNameWebsite-140">\n         [140]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       It was launched 26 November 2011, and landed at\n       <a href="/wiki/Gale_(crater)" title="Gale (crater)">\n        Gale Crater\n       </a>\n       on 6 August 2012.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Gale_Crater3_39-1">\n        <a href="#cite_note-Gale_Crater3-39">\n         [39]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       Mission objectives are to help assess Mars\'\n       <a href="/wiki/Planetary_habitability" title="Planetary habitability">\n        habitability\n       </a>\n       and in doing so, determine whether Mars is or has ever been able to support\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Life_on_Mars_(planet)" title="Life on Mars (planet)">\n        life\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-MSL-main_page_141-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-MSL-main_page-141">\n         [141]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       collect data for a future\n       <a href="/wiki/Human_mission_to_Mars" title="Human mission to Mars">\n        human mission\n       </a>\n       , study Martian geology, its climate, and further assess the role that\n       <a href="/wiki/Water_on_Mars" title="Water on Mars">\n        water\n       </a>\n       , an essential ingredient for life as we know it, played in forming minerals on Mars.\n      </p>\n      <h3>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Tanpopo">\n        Tanpopo\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Astrobiology&amp;action=edit&amp;section=19" title="Edit section: Tanpopo">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <div class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable" role="note">\n       Main article:\n       <a href="/wiki/Tanpopo_(mission)" title="Tanpopo (mission)">\n        Tanpopo (mission)\n       </a>\n      </div>\n      <p>\n       The\n       <a href="/wiki/Tanpopo_(mission)" title="Tanpopo (mission)">\n        Tanpopo\n       </a>\n       mission is an orbital astrobiology experiment investigating the potential interplanetary transfer of life,\n       <a href="/wiki/Organic_compound" title="Organic compound">\n        organic compounds\n       </a>\n       , and possible terrestrial particles in the low Earth orbit. The purpose is to assess the\n       <a href="/wiki/Panspermia" title="Panspermia">\n        panspermia\n       </a>\n       hypothesis and the possibility of natural interplanetary transport of microbial life as well as prebiotic organic compounds. Early mission results show evidence that some clumps of microorganism can survive for at least one year in space.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-AGU2017_142-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-AGU2017-142">\n         [142]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       This may support the idea that clumps greater than 0.5 millimeters of microorganisms could be one way for life to spread from planet to planet.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-AGU2017_142-1">\n        <a href="#cite_note-AGU2017-142">\n         [142]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <h3>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="ExoMars_rover">\n        ExoMars rover\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Astrobiology&amp;action=edit&amp;section=20" title="Edit section: ExoMars rover">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <div class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable" role="note">\n       Main article:\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/ExoMars_rover" title="ExoMars rover">\n        ExoMars rover\n       </a>\n      </div>\n      <div class="thumb tright">\n       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;">\n        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:ExoMars_model_at_ILA_2006.jpg">\n         <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="1440" data-file-width="2160" height="147" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/46/ExoMars_model_at_ILA_2006.jpg/220px-ExoMars_model_at_ILA_2006.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/46/ExoMars_model_at_ILA_2006.jpg/330px-ExoMars_model_at_ILA_2006.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/46/ExoMars_model_at_ILA_2006.jpg/440px-ExoMars_model_at_ILA_2006.jpg 2x" width="220"/>\n        </a>\n        <div class="thumbcaption">\n         <div class="magnify">\n          <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:ExoMars_model_at_ILA_2006.jpg" title="Enlarge">\n          </a>\n         </div>\n         ExoMars rover model\n        </div>\n       </div>\n      </div>\n      <p>\n       ExoMars is a robotic mission to Mars to search for possible\n       <a href="/wiki/Biosignature" title="Biosignature">\n        biosignatures\n       </a>\n       of\n       <a href="/wiki/Life_on_Mars" title="Life on Mars">\n        Martian life\n       </a>\n       , past or present. This astrobiological mission is currently under development by the\n       <a href="/wiki/European_Space_Agency" title="European Space Agency">\n        European Space Agency\n       </a>\n       (ESA) in partnership with the\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Russian_Federal_Space_Agency" title="Russian Federal Space Agency">\n        Russian Federal Space Agency\n       </a>\n       (Roscosmos); it is planned for a 2018 launch.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-still_keen_143-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-still_keen-143">\n         [143]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Svitak_144-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-Svitak-144">\n         [144]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Selding_145-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-Selding-145">\n         [145]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <h3>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Mars_2020">\n        Mars 2020\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Astrobiology&amp;action=edit&amp;section=21" title="Edit section: Mars 2020">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <div class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable" role="note">\n       Main article:\n       <a href="/wiki/Mars_2020" title="Mars 2020">\n        Mars 2020\n       </a>\n      </div>\n      <p>\n       The \'Mars 2020\' rover mission is a concept under development by NASA with a possible launch in 2020. It is intended to investigate environments on Mars relevant to astrobiology, investigate its surface\n       <a href="/wiki/Geology_of_Mars" title="Geology of Mars">\n        geological processes\n       </a>\n       and history, including the assessment of its past\n       <a href="/wiki/Planetary_habitability" title="Planetary habitability">\n        habitability\n       </a>\n       and potential for preservation of\n       <a href="/wiki/Biosignature" title="Biosignature">\n        biosignatures\n       </a>\n       and\n       <a href="/wiki/Biomolecule" title="Biomolecule">\n        biomolecules\n       </a>\n       within accessible geological materials.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Cowing_146-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-Cowing-146">\n         [146]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       The Science Definition Team is proposing the rover collect and package at least 31 samples of rock cores and soil for a later mission to bring back for more definitive analysis in laboratories on Earth. The rover could make measurements and technology demonstrations to help designers of a\n       <a href="/wiki/Human_mission_to_Mars" title="Human mission to Mars">\n        human expedition\n       </a>\n       understand any hazards posed by Martian dust and demonstrate how to collect\n       <a href="/wiki/Carbon_dioxide" title="Carbon dioxide">\n        carbon dioxide\n       </a>\n       (CO\n       <sub>\n        2\n       </sub>\n       ), which could be a resource for making molecular oxygen (O\n       <sub>\n        2\n       </sub>\n       ) and\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Rocket_fuel" title="Rocket fuel">\n        rocket fuel\n       </a>\n       .\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-goals_147-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-goals-147">\n         [147]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-FAQ_148-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-FAQ-148">\n         [148]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <h3>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Europa_Clipper">\n        Europa Clipper\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Astrobiology&amp;action=edit&amp;section=22" title="Edit section: Europa Clipper">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <div class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable" role="note">\n       Main article:\n       <a href="/wiki/Europa_Clipper" title="Europa Clipper">\n        Europa Clipper\n       </a>\n      </div>\n      <p>\n       Europa Clipper is a mission planned by NASA for a 2025 launch that will conduct detailed reconnaissance of\n       <a href="/wiki/Jupiter" title="Jupiter">\n        Jupiter\n       </a>\n       \'s moon\n       <a href="/wiki/Europa_(moon)" title="Europa (moon)">\n        Europa\n       </a>\n       and will investigate whether the icy moon could harbor conditions suitable for life.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-missions_149-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-missions-149">\n         [149]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-FPE_150-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-FPE-150">\n         [150]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       It will also aid in the selection of future\n       <a href="/wiki/Lander_(spacecraft)" title="Lander (spacecraft)">\n        landing sites\n       </a>\n       .\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Europa_Lander_2013_151-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-Europa_Lander_2013-151">\n         [151]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-152">\n        <a href="#cite_note-152">\n         [152]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <h3>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Proposed_concepts">\n        Proposed concepts\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Astrobiology&amp;action=edit&amp;section=23" title="Edit section: Proposed concepts">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h3>\n      <h4>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Icebreaker_Life">\n        Icebreaker Life\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Astrobiology&amp;action=edit&amp;section=24" title="Edit section: Icebreaker Life">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h4>\n      <div class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable" role="note">\n       Main article:\n       <a href="/wiki/Icebreaker_Life" title="Icebreaker Life">\n        Icebreaker Life\n       </a>\n      </div>\n      <p>\n       <i>\n        Icebreaker Life\n       </i>\n       is a lander mission that proposed for NASA\'s\n       <a href="/wiki/Discovery_Program" title="Discovery Program">\n        Discovery Program\n       </a>\n       for the 2021 launch opportunity,\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Icebreaker2021_153-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-Icebreaker2021-153">\n         [153]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       but it was not selected for development. It would have had a stationary lander that would be a near copy of the successful 2008\n       <a href="/wiki/Phoenix_(spacecraft)" title="Phoenix (spacecraft)">\n        <i>\n         Phoenix\n        </i>\n       </a>\n       and it would have carried an upgraded astrobiology scientific payload, including a 1-meter-long core drill to sample ice-cemented ground in the northern plains to conduct a search for\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Organic_molecule" title="Organic molecule">\n        organic molecules\n       </a>\n       and evidence of current or past\n       <a href="/wiki/Life_on_Mars" title="Life on Mars">\n        life on Mars\n       </a>\n       .\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-AstrobioMag_154-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-AstrobioMag-154">\n         [154]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-LPI_2012_155-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-LPI_2012-155">\n         [155]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       One of the key goals of the\n       <i>\n        Icebreaker Life\n       </i>\n       mission is to test the\n       <a href="/wiki/Hypothesis" title="Hypothesis">\n        hypothesis\n       </a>\n       that the ice-rich ground in the polar regions has significant concentrations of organics due to protection by the ice from\n       <a href="/wiki/Oxidizing_agent" title="Oxidizing agent">\n        oxidants\n       </a>\n       and\n       <a href="/wiki/Sunlight" title="Sunlight">\n        radiation\n       </a>\n       .\n      </p>\n      <h4>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Journey_to_Enceladus_and_Titan">\n        Journey to Enceladus and Titan\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Astrobiology&amp;action=edit&amp;section=25" title="Edit section: Journey to Enceladus and Titan">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h4>\n      <p>\n       <a href="/wiki/Journey_to_Enceladus_and_Titan" title="Journey to Enceladus and Titan">\n        Journey to Enceladus and Titan\n       </a>\n       (JET) is an orbiter astrobiology mission concept to assess the\n       <a href="/wiki/Planetary_habitability" title="Planetary habitability">\n        habitability\n       </a>\n       potential of\n       <a href="/wiki/Saturn" title="Saturn">\n        Saturn\n       </a>\n       \'s moons\n       <a href="/wiki/Enceladus" title="Enceladus">\n        Enceladus\n       </a>\n       and\n       <a href="/wiki/Titan_(moon)" title="Titan (moon)">\n        Titan\n       </a>\n       .\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Sotin2011_156-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-Sotin2011-156">\n         [156]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-JET_204_157-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-JET_204-157">\n         [157]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-LCPM-2013_158-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-LCPM-2013-158">\n         [158]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <h4>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Enceladus_Life_Finder">\n        Enceladus Life Finder\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Astrobiology&amp;action=edit&amp;section=26" title="Edit section: Enceladus Life Finder">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h4>\n      <p>\n       <a href="/wiki/Enceladus_Life_Finder" title="Enceladus Life Finder">\n        Enceladus Life Finder\n       </a>\n       (ELF) is a proposed astrobiology mission concept for a space probe intended to assess the\n       <a href="/wiki/Planetary_habitability" title="Planetary habitability">\n        habitability\n       </a>\n       of the\n       <a href="/wiki/Extraterrestrial_liquid_water#Enceladus" title="Extraterrestrial liquid water">\n        internal aquatic ocean\n       </a>\n       of\n       <a href="/wiki/Enceladus" title="Enceladus">\n        Enceladus\n       </a>\n       ,\n       <a href="/wiki/Saturn" title="Saturn">\n        Saturn\n       </a>\n       \'s\n       <a href="/wiki/Moons_of_Saturn" title="Moons of Saturn">\n        sixth-largest moon\n       </a>\n       .\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-2015_LPSC_159-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-2015_LPSC-159">\n         [159]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-contestants_160-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-contestants-160">\n         [160]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <h4>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Life_Investigation_For_Enceladus">\n        Life Investigation For Enceladus\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Astrobiology&amp;action=edit&amp;section=27" title="Edit section: Life Investigation For Enceladus">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h4>\n      <p>\n       <a href="/wiki/Life_Investigation_For_Enceladus" title="Life Investigation For Enceladus">\n        Life Investigation For Enceladus\n       </a>\n       (LIFE) is a proposed astrobiology sample-return mission concept. The spacecraft would enter into\n       <a href="/wiki/Saturn" title="Saturn">\n        Saturn\n       </a>\n       orbit and enable multiple flybys through Enceladus\' icy plumes to collect icy plume particles and volatiles and return them to Earth on a capsule. The spacecraft may sample Enceladus\' plumes, the\n       <a href="/wiki/Rings_of_Saturn#E_Ring" title="Rings of Saturn">\n        E ring of Saturn\n       </a>\n       , and the upper atmosphere of\n       <a href="/wiki/Titan_(moon)" title="Titan (moon)">\n        Titan\n       </a>\n       .\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Astro2012_161-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-Astro2012-161">\n         [161]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Porco_2014_162-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-Porco_2014-162">\n         [162]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Doc_2013_163-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-Doc_2013-163">\n         [163]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <h4>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Oceanus">\n        Oceanus\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Astrobiology&amp;action=edit&amp;section=28" title="Edit section: Oceanus">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h4>\n      <div class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable" role="note">\n       Main article:\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Oceanus_Mission" title="Oceanus Mission">\n        Oceanus Mission\n       </a>\n      </div>\n      <p>\n       <i>\n        Oceanus\n       </i>\n       is an orbiter proposed in 2017 for the\n       <a href="/wiki/New_Frontiers_program" title="New Frontiers program">\n        New Frontiers\n       </a>\n       mission #4. It would travel to the moon of\n       <a href="/wiki/Saturn" title="Saturn">\n        Saturn\n       </a>\n       -\n       <a href="/wiki/Titan_(moon)" title="Titan (moon)">\n        Titan\n       </a>\n       , to assess its\n       <a href="/wiki/Planetary_habitability" title="Planetary habitability">\n        habitability\n       </a>\n       .\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-sotin_164-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-sotin-164">\n         [164]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n       <i>\n        Oceanus\n       </i>\n       objectives are to reveal Titan\'s\n       <a href="/wiki/Organic_chemistry" title="Organic chemistry">\n        organic chemistry\n       </a>\n       , geology, gravity, topography, collect 3D reconnaissance data, catalog the\n       <a href="/wiki/Organic_compound" title="Organic compound">\n        organics\n       </a>\n       and determine where they may interact with liquid water.\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-165">\n        <a href="#cite_note-165">\n         [165]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <h4>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="Explorer_of_Enceladus_and_Titan">\n        Explorer of Enceladus and Titan\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         [\n        </span>\n        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Astrobiology&amp;action=edit&amp;section=29" title="Edit section: Explorer of Enceladus and Titan">\n         edit\n        </a>\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n         ]\n        </span>\n       </span>\n      </h4>\n      <div class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable" role="note">\n       Main article:\n       <a href="/wiki/Explorer_of_Enceladus_and_Titan" title="Explorer of Enceladus and Titan">\n        Explorer of Enceladus and Titan\n       </a>\n      </div>\n      <p>\n       <i>\n        Explorer of Enceladus and Titan\n       </i>\n       is an orbiter mission concept that would investigate the evolution and\n       <a href="/wiki/Planetary_habitability" title="Planetary habitability">\n        habitability\n       </a>\n       of the Saturnian satellites\n       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Enceladus_(moon)" title="Enceladus (moon)">\n        Enceladus\n       </a>\n       and\n       <a href="/wiki/Titan_(moon)" title="Titan (moon)">\n        Titan\n       </a>\n       and was proposed in 2017 by the\n       <a href="/wiki/European_Space_Agency" title="European Space Agency">\n        European Space Agency\n       </a>\n       .\n       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-E2T_2017_166-0">\n        <a href="#cite_note-E2T_2017-166">\n         [166]\n        </a>\n       </sup>\n      </p>\n      <h2>\n       <span class="mw-headline" id="See_also">\n        See also\n       </span>\n       <span class="mw-editsection">\n        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">\n
